(function() {
    /*
    |--------------------------------------------------------------------------
    | PRELOAD
    |--------------------------------------------------------------------------
    */
    var preloadInit = function() {
        if(localStorage.alreadyVisited){
            $("#preload-wrapper").hide();
        }
        else{
            localStorage.alreadyVisited = true;
            if ($("#preload-wrapper").length) {
                preloadStart();
            }
        }
    }

    var preloadStart = function(start) {
        var PathLoader = function(el) {
            this.el = el;
            // clear stroke
            this.el.style.strokeDasharray = this.el.style.strokeDashoffset = this.el.getTotalLength();
        }
        PathLoader.prototype._draw = function(val) {
            this.el.style.strokeDashoffset = this.el.getTotalLength() * (1 - val);
        }
        PathLoader.prototype.setProgress = function(val) {
            this._draw(val);
        }
        PathLoader.prototype.setProgressFn = function(fn) {
            if (typeof fn === 'function') {
                fn(this);
            }
        }

        var progress = 0
        var simulationFn = function(instance) {
            var interval = setInterval(function() {
                progress = Math.min(progress + Math.random() * 0.1, 1);
                instance.setProgress(progress);

                // reached the end
                if (progress === 1) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    preloadEnd();
                }
            }, 100);
        };

        var loaderInnerCircle = $("#preload-loader-circle");
        var loader = new PathLoader(loaderInnerCircle[0]);

        $(document).on("animationend webkitAnimationEnd", "#preload-wrapper .loader", function(event) {
            if (event.originalEvent.animationName == "animInitialHeader") {
                start = false;
                loader.setProgressFn(simulationFn);
            }
            if (event.originalEvent.animationName == "animLoadedLoader") {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $("#preload-wrapper").hide();
                }, 200)
            }
        });

        if (start) {
            progress = 0;
            loader.setProgressFn(simulationFn);
        }
    }

    var preloadEnd = function() {
        var preloadWrapper = $("#preload-wrapper");
        preloadWrapper.removeClass("loading").addClass("loaded");
    }

    preloadInit();
})();
